43a5(kha'o): rkyen gyis bar du gcod pa'i mig las sprul pa'i rnam grangs/ phyi snod kyi/ nang bcud kyi/ rang bzhin gyis 'byung ba'i/ byed pa pos byas pa'i/ po'i/ mo'i/ ma zhing gi/ rgas pa'i/ 
43a6(kha'o): gzhon nu'i/ zha grum du gyur pa'i gzugs las sprul pa'i rnam grangs/ lha'i rna ba yongs su tshangs pas/ yid kyi sgra thos pa/ lha'i rna ba don gyi tshangs pas gsang ba'i sgra thos pa// 
43b1(kha'o): lha'i rna ba rang gi tshangs pas snang srid kyi sgra thos pa/ lha'i rna ba rang bzhin gyi tshangs pas dus kyi sgra thos pa/ lha'i rna ba ngo bo nyid tshangs pas srid gsum gyi sgra thes pa/ lha'i rna ba yid / 
43b2(kha'o): bzhin gyi tshangs pas khams gsum gyi sgra thos pa/ gdos pa can gyi rna ba yongs su tshangs pas gyur pa zab mo'i sgra thos pa/ gdos pa can gyi rna ba don gyi tshangs pas thun mong gi / 
43b3(kha'o): sgra thos pa/ gdos pa can gyi rna ba ngang gi tshangs pas du ti'i sgra thos pa/ gdos pa can gyi rna ba rang bzhin gyi tshangs pas pra mo ha'i sgra thos pa/ gdos pa can gyi rna ba ngo bo nyid kyi 
43b4(kha'o): tshangs pas rtags kyi sgra thos pa/ gdos pa can gyi rna ba yid bzhin gyi tshangs pas bya sang khri ta la sogs te sems can thams cad kyi sgra thos pa/ gdes pa can gyi rna ba yongs su 
43b5(kha'o): tshangs pas bden pa'i sgra thos pa/ gds pa can gyi rna brkyen gyis bar du gcod pa las spul pa'i rnam grangs/ phyi'/ nang gi/ srid pa'i/ bskal pa'i/ tsha grang 'thab pa'i/ rlung 
43b6(kha'o): g.yo ba'i/ me g.yo ba'i/ chu g.yo ba'i/ sa g.yo ba'i/ lha srin 'thab pa'i/ sems can gyi/ rang bzhin gyi/ byed pa pos byas pa'i sgra las sprul pa'i rnam grangs/ lha'i sna 
44a1(kha'o): rnam par ma 'gags pas/ snang rid kyi ri tsher bg/ lha'i sna mngon par ma 'gags pas thams gsum gyi ro tsher ba/ ha'i sna rang bzhin gyi ma 'gags pa rig / 
44a2(kha'o): 'dzin gye dro sor b/ lha'i na yed bzhin gyi ma 'gags pas zab bo'i ro tshe ba/ lha'i sdang bo nyid kyi ma 'gags pa 'lhyi bthan gyi dro tsoMr ba/ bha'i sna yongs su ma 'gags
44a3(kha'o): pas sa 'og ma na gnas pa'i dro tsor ba/ lha'i na shin tu ma 'gags pas gnas 'og ma nas mi gtsang ba 'byung ba'i dri tsher ba/ 'gog pa can gyi snas dpag tshad lnga brgya byed dang

44b1(kha'o): bsngal 'byung ba'i dri tsher ba'i sna las sprul pa'i rnam grangs/ snang srid kyi sri/ khams gsum gyi/ rig 'dzin/ zab mo'i/ spyi mthun gyi/ sa 'og ma na gnas pa'i/ gnas 
44b2(kha'o): 'og ma nas mi gtsang 'byung ba'i/ nad dang dug gi/ srid pa brlan gyi/ bskal pa g.yo ba'i/ rlangs dang d kyi mchod pa'i/ gsur gzob kyi/ bag chags kyi/ yasg bar phan tshun 
44b3(kha'o): gyi/ thad du 'byung ba'i/ mi mthun pa'i/ tshang stangs kyi dre las spul pa'i rnam grangs/ lha'i the rnam par grol bas id gsum gyi kha lo bsgyur bar smra ba/ lha'i lce mngon par grol

44b5(kha'o): brta chig ston par mdzad pa/ lha'i lo ngo bo nyid kyi grol bas spyi bthun pa'i brda' so sor ston cing kha lo bsgyur ba/ lha'i lce yongs su grol bas sa 'og ma na gnas pa'i gong mar 
44b6(kha'o): 'gro ba'i brta tshig kha lo bsgyur ba/ lha'i lce zhin tu grol bas drug bdud rtsir bsgyur ba'i ro gtong ba/ de ltar na/ lha'i les yid la bsgyur ba'i brda' sprad pa/ lha ma yin gyi / 
45a1(kha'o): lces ngag 'khyal pa dang tshig rlub ba r smra ba/ mi'i les brta skad tsho dgu rigs mi mthun par bsgyur ba/ byil song gi les khyu rigs dang sde tshan bsgyur ba/ yi dgas

45a3(kha'o): gcod pa'i the las sprul pa'i rnam grangs/ yid bzhin gyi/ sprul pa'i/ bdud rtsi'/ lha shings lu lta bu gtsang ma'i/ srid pa 'od kyi mtsho lta bu'i/ zas dkar gyi 'dod 'dzo' ba dang /

45a5(kha'o): ha ra bta'/ rtsi nyamng brgya stab sbyor gyi/ la min dang / shing tog gi/ skyed mo' tshal gyi/ rtsi tog ldam 'byung gi/ shing skye ba mo tsam las byung ba'i/ rdo yar mo la ka las

45b1(kha'o): las sprul pa'i rnam grangs/ srid pa gsum la dbang bsgyur ba lus dpag tshad brgyad khri bzhi stong du sprul nus pa yod do// 'jig rten gcig la dbang bsgyur ba lus dpag tshad nyis

45b3(kha'o): zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad dgu stong drug brgya ru sprul nus pa yod d// gya nom snang ba'i lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad bzhi stong brgyad brgya spul nus pa yod do// shin tu mthong ba'i

45b5(kha'o): zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad drug brgya run spul nus pa yod do// 'bras bu che ba'i lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad sum brgya ru sul nus pa yod do// bsod nams skye ba'i lha zhes bya 
45b6(kha'o): ba lus dpag tshad gnyis brgya lnga bcu ru sprul nus pa yod do// sprin med 'od kyi lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga ru sprul nus pa yod do// tshad med dge ba'i lha 
46a1(kha'o): zhes bya ba lus dpag chad drug hu rtsa bzhi ran sprul nus pa yod d// dge rgyas kyi lha zhes bya ba lus dpag cshad sdum hu rtsa gnyis su sprul nus pa yod d// dge chung 
46a2(kha'o): gi lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad bcu drug tu sprul nus pa yod do// tshad med 'od kyi lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad brgyad du sprul nus pa yod do// 'od gsal gyi lha zhes bya ba lus 
46a3(kha'o): dpag tshad bzhi ru sprul nus pa yod do// 'od chung gi lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad gnyis su sprul nus pa yod do// tshangs pa 'bum khri' lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad byed dang / 
46a4(kha'o): gnyis su sprul nus pa yod d// tshangs pa kun 'khor gyi lha zhes bya ba lus dpag tshad gcig tu spul nus pa yod d// tshangs pa mdun na 'don pa'i lha zhes bya ba lus dpag

46a6(kha'o): bzhi pa'i lus blangs pa la spul nus pa yod do// 'phrul dga'i lha zhes bya ba rgyang grags gnyis pa'i lus blangs pa la spul nus pa yod do// dga' ldan gyi lha zhes bya ba rgyang 
46b1(kha'o): grags gcig pa'i lus blangs pa la spul nus pa yod do// sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha zhes bya ba rgyang grags pbyed pa'i lus blangs pa la sprul nus pa yod do// rgyal chen rigs /

46b3(kha'o): gnod sbyin gyi snde tshogs zhes bya ba khu brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga pa'i lus blangs pa la spul nus pa yod d// klu mud zangs kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba khu drug cu rtsa byed dang / gsum gyi lus 
46b4(kha'o): blangs pa la spul nus pa yod do// de ltar na/ mi'i lus khru sum su rtsa gnyis la spul nus pa yod do// mi'i lus khru bcu drug pa/ mi'i lus khru brgyad pa/ mi'i lus khru bzhi /
